## currency settler BaseOverrideFee

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {BaseOverrideFee} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/fee/BaseOverrideFee.sol";␊
    import {Currency} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/Currency.sol";␊
    import {CurrencySettler} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/utils/CurrencySettler.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    ␊
    // TODO: Override \`_getFee\` to customize the swap fee for each swap␊
    // i.e. dynamic fees depending on current market conditions, swap size, swap direction, etc␊
    contract MyHook is BaseOverrideFee, ERC20 {␊
        using CurrencySettler for Currency;␊
    ␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager)␊
            BaseHook(_poolManager)␊
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")␊
        {}␊
    ␊
        function _getFee(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (uint24)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the LP fee is computed␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96, int24 tick)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeDonate␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: false,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: false,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: false,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: false,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: false␊
            });␊
        }␊
    }␊
    `

## safeCast BaseOverrideFee

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {BaseOverrideFee} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/fee/BaseOverrideFee.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {SafeCast} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/utils/math/SafeCast.sol";␊
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    ␊
    // TODO: Override \`_getFee\` to customize the swap fee for each swap␊
    // i.e. dynamic fees depending on current market conditions, swap size, swap direction, etc␊
    contract MyHook is BaseOverrideFee, ERC20 {␊
        using SafeCast for *;␊
    ␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager)␊
            BaseHook(_poolManager)␊
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")␊
        {}␊
    ␊
        function _getFee(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (uint24)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the LP fee is computed␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96, int24 tick)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeDonate␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: false,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: false,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: false,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: false,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: false␊
            });␊
        }␊
    }␊
    `

## transient storage BaseOverrideFee

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {BaseOverrideFee} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/fee/BaseOverrideFee.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {SlotDerivation} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/utils/SlotDerivation.sol";␊
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {TransientSlot} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/utils/TransientSlot.sol";␊
    ␊
    // TODO: Override \`_getFee\` to customize the swap fee for each swap␊
    // i.e. dynamic fees depending on current market conditions, swap size, swap direction, etc␊
    contract MyHook is BaseOverrideFee, ERC20 {␊
        using SlotDerivation for bytes32;␊
        using TransientSlot for bytes32;␊
    ␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager)␊
            BaseHook(_poolManager)␊
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")␊
        {}␊
    ␊
        function _getFee(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (uint24)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the LP fee is computed␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96, int24 tick)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeDonate␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: false,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: false,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: false,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: false,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: false␊
            });␊
        }␊
    }␊
    `

## access control (ownable) BaseOverrideFee

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {BaseOverrideFee} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/fee/BaseOverrideFee.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {Ownable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    ␊
    // TODO: Override \`_getFee\` to customize the swap fee for each swap␊
    // i.e. dynamic fees depending on current market conditions, swap size, swap direction, etc␊
    contract MyHook is BaseOverrideFee, Ownable, ERC20 {␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address initialOwner)␊
            BaseHook(_poolManager)␊
            Ownable(initialOwner)␊
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")␊
        {}␊
    ␊
        function _getFee(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (uint24)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the LP fee is computed␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96, int24 tick)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeDonate␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: false,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: false,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: false,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: false,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: false␊
            });␊
        }␊
    }␊

## access control (roles) BaseOverrideFee

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {AccessControl} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/AccessControl.sol";␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {BaseOverrideFee} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/fee/BaseOverrideFee.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    ␊
    // TODO: Override \`_getFee\` to customize the swap fee for each swap␊
    // i.e. dynamic fees depending on current market conditions, swap size, swap direction, etc␊
    contract MyHook is BaseOverrideFee, AccessControl, ERC20 {␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address defaultAdmin)␊
            BaseHook(_poolManager)␊
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")␊
        {␊
            _grantRole(DEFAULT_ADMIN_ROLE, defaultAdmin);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _getFee(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (uint24)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the LP fee is computed␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96, int24 tick)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeDonate␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: false,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: false,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: false,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: false,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: false␊
            });␊
        }␊
    }␊
    `

## access control (managed) BaseOverrideFee

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {AccessManaged} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/manager/AccessManaged.sol";␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {BaseOverrideFee} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/fee/BaseOverrideFee.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊

    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    ␊
    // TODO: Override \`_getFee\` to customize the swap fee for each swap␊
    // i.e. dynamic fees depending on current market conditions, swap size, swap direction, etc␊
    contract MyHook is BaseOverrideFee, AccessManaged, ERC20 {␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address initialAuthority)␊
            BaseHook(_poolManager)␊
            AccessManaged(initialAuthority)␊
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")␊
        {}␊
    ␊
        function _getFee(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊

        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊

            // TODO: Implement __beforeAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeDonate␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: false,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: false,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: false,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: false,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: false␊
            });␊
        }␊
    }␊

## pausable BaseOverrideFee

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {BaseOverrideFee} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/fee/BaseOverrideFee.sol";␊
    import {BeforeSwapDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BeforeSwapDelta.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {Ownable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable.sol";␊
    import {Pausable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/utils/Pausable.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    ␊
    // TODO: Override \`_getFee\` to customize the swap fee for each swap␊
    // i.e. dynamic fees depending on current market conditions, swap size, swap direction, etc␊
    contract MyHook is BaseOverrideFee, ERC20, Pausable, Ownable {␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address initialOwner)␊
            BaseHook(_poolManager)␊
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")␊
            Ownable(initialOwner)␊
        {}␊
    ␊
        function _getFee(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (uint24)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the LP fee is computed␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function pause() public onlyOwner {␊
            _pause();␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function unpause() public onlyOwner {␊
            _unpause();␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            return super._beforeAddLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            return super._beforeRemoveLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)␊
        {␊
            return super._beforeSwap(sender, key, params, hookData);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            return super._beforeDonate(sender, key, amount0, amount1, hookData);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96, int24 tick)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: false,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: false,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: false,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: false,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: false␊
            });␊
        }␊
    }␊
    `

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊

    ␊
    // TODO: Override \`_getFee\` to customize the swap fee for each swap␊
    // i.e. dynamic fees depending on current market conditions, swap size, swap direction, etc␊
    contract MyHook is BaseOverrideFee, ERC20 {␊

## basic BaseDynamicAfterFee

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";␊
    import {BaseDynamicAfterFee} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/fee/BaseDynamicAfterFee.sol";␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    ␊
    // TODO: Override \`_getTargetUnspecified\` to customize the swap outcome target␊
    // i.e. capture any positive difference of the swap outcome that surpasses the target␊
    contract MyHook is BaseDynamicAfterFee, ERC20 {␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager)␊
            BaseHook(_poolManager)␊
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")␊
        {}␊
    ␊
        function _getTargetUnspecified(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (uint256, bool)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the target unspecified amount is computed␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterSwapHandler(PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta, uint256 targetUnspecifiedAmount, uint256 feeAmount)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the accumulated target penalty fees are handled after swaps␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96, int24 tick)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeDonate␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: false,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: true,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: false,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: false␊
            });␊
        }␊
    }␊

## mixed permissions BaseDynamicAfterFee

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊

        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeDonate␊

    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊

        {␊

                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: false,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊

            override␊

            // TODO: Implement how the accumulated target penalty fees are handled after swaps␊
        }␊

        }␊
    ␊

            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta0, BalanceDelta delta1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, BalanceDelta)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterDonate␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: false,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: false,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: false,␊

                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: true␊

        }␊
    }␊
    `

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊

    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊

        }␊

                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊

                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: false␊

## access control (roles) BaseDynamicAfterFee

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {AccessControl} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/AccessControl.sol";␊
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";␊
    import {BaseDynamicAfterFee} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/fee/BaseDynamicAfterFee.sol";␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊

    ␊
    // TODO: Override \`_getTargetUnspecified\` to customize the swap outcome target␊

        }␊

        }␊
    ␊

## pausable BaseDynamicAfterFee

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";␊
    import {BaseDynamicAfterFee} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/fee/BaseDynamicAfterFee.sol";␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {BeforeSwapDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BeforeSwapDelta.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {Ownable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable.sol";␊
    import {Pausable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/utils/Pausable.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    ␊
    // TODO: Override \`_getTargetUnspecified\` to customize the swap outcome target␊
    // i.e. capture any positive difference of the swap outcome that surpasses the target␊
    contract MyHook is BaseDynamicAfterFee, ERC20, Pausable, Ownable {␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address initialOwner)␊
            BaseHook(_poolManager)␊
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")␊
            Ownable(initialOwner)␊
        {}␊
    ␊
        function _getTargetUnspecified(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (uint256, bool)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the target unspecified amount is computed␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterSwapHandler(PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta, uint256 targetUnspecifiedAmount, uint256 feeAmount)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the accumulated target penalty fees are handled after swaps␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function pause() public onlyOwner {␊
            _pause();␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function unpause() public onlyOwner {␊
            _unpause();␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            return super._beforeAddLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            return super._beforeRemoveLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)␊
        {␊
            return super._beforeSwap(sender, key, params, hookData);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            return super._beforeDonate(sender, key, amount0, amount1, hookData);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96, int24 tick)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: false,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: true,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: false,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: false␊
            });␊
        }␊
    }␊
    `

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";␊
    import {BaseDynamicAfterFee} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/fee/BaseDynamicAfterFee.sol";␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {ERC1155} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC1155/ERC1155.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    ␊
    // TODO: Override \`_getTargetUnspecified\` to customize the swap outcome target␊
    // i.e. capture any positive difference of the swap outcome that surpasses the target␊
    contract MyHook is BaseDynamicAfterFee, ERC1155 {␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager)␊
            BaseHook(_poolManager)␊
            ERC1155("https://example.com/metadata/{id}.json")␊
        {}␊
    ␊
        function _getTargetUnspecified(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (uint256, bool)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the target unspecified amount is computed␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterSwapHandler(PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta, uint256 targetUnspecifiedAmount, uint256 feeAmount)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the accumulated target penalty fees are handled after swaps␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96, int24 tick)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeDonate␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: false,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: true,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: false,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: false␊
            });␊
        }␊
    }␊
    `

## basic BaseHookFee

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {BaseHookFee} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/fee/BaseHookFee.sol";␊
    import {BeforeSwapDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BeforeSwapDelta.sol";␊
    import {Currency} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/Currency.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    ␊
    // TODO: Override \`_getHookFee\` to customize the hook fee collection for the entire pool␊
    // i.e. dynamic hook-owned fees depending on current market conditions, etc␊
    contract MyHook is BaseHookFee, ERC20 {␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager)␊
            BaseHook(_poolManager)␊
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")␊
        {}␊
    ␊
        function _getHookFee(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            view␊
            override␊
            returns (uint24)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the Hook fee is computed␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function handleHookFees(Currency[] memory currencies) public override {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the accumulated hook fees are handled␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96, int24 tick)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeSwap␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeDonate␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: false,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: true,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊

                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,␊

        {}␊
    ␊
        function _getHookFee(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            view␊
            override␊
            returns (uint24)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the Hook fee is computed␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function handleHookFees(Currency[] memory currencies) public override {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the accumulated hook fees are handled␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96, int24 tick)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta0, BalanceDelta delta1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, BalanceDelta)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta0, BalanceDelta delta1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊

            returns (bytes4, BalanceDelta)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeSwap␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeDonate␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterDonate␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: true,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: true,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: true␊
            });␊
        }␊
    }␊

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";␊

            // TODO: Implement __beforeInitialize␊

        }␊

                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: false␊
            });␊
        }␊
    }␊
    `

## access control (roles) BaseHookFee

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {AccessControl} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/AccessControl.sol";␊
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {BaseHookFee} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/fee/BaseHookFee.sol";␊
    import {BeforeSwapDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BeforeSwapDelta.sol";␊
    import {Currency} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/Currency.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    ␊
    // TODO: Override \`_getHookFee\` to customize the hook fee collection for the entire pool␊
    // i.e. dynamic hook-owned fees depending on current market conditions, etc␊
    contract MyHook is BaseHookFee, AccessControl, ERC20 {␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address defaultAdmin)␊
            BaseHook(_poolManager)␊
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")␊
        {␊
            _grantRole(DEFAULT_ADMIN_ROLE, defaultAdmin);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _getHookFee(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            view␊
            override␊
            returns (uint24)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the Hook fee is computed␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function handleHookFees(Currency[] memory currencies) public override {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the accumulated hook fees are handled␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96, int24 tick)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeSwap␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeDonate␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: false,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: true,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: false,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: false␊
            });␊
        }␊
    }␊

## pausable BaseHookFee

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {BaseHookFee} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/fee/BaseHookFee.sol";␊
    import {BeforeSwapDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BeforeSwapDelta.sol";␊
    import {Currency} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/Currency.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {Ownable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable.sol";␊
    import {Pausable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/utils/Pausable.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    ␊
    // TODO: Override \`_getHookFee\` to customize the hook fee collection for the entire pool␊
    // i.e. dynamic hook-owned fees depending on current market conditions, etc␊
    contract MyHook is BaseHookFee, ERC20, Pausable, Ownable {␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address initialOwner)␊
            BaseHook(_poolManager)␊
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")␊
            Ownable(initialOwner)␊
        {}␊
    ␊
        function _getHookFee(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            view␊
            override␊
            returns (uint24)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the Hook fee is computed␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function handleHookFees(Currency[] memory currencies)␊
            public␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the accumulated hook fees are handled␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function pause() public onlyOwner {␊
            _pause();␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function unpause() public onlyOwner {␊
            _unpause();␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            return super._beforeAddLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            return super._beforeRemoveLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)␊
        {␊
            return super._beforeSwap(sender, key, params, hookData);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            return super._beforeDonate(sender, key, amount0, amount1, hookData);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96, int24 tick)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: false,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: true,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: false,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: false␊
            });␊
        }␊
    }␊

            override␊
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeSwap␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeDonate␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: false,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: true,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: false,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: false,␊

## shares erc6909 BaseHookFee

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊

    import {BeforeSwapDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BeforeSwapDelta.sol";␊
    import {Currency} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/Currency.sol";␊

            // TODO: Implement __beforeInitialize␊

            internal␊

        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊

## basic AntiSandwichHook

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {AntiSandwichHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/general/AntiSandwichHook.sol";␊
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    ␊
    // TODO: Override \`_afterSwapHandler\` to determine how accumulated penalty fees are handled␊
    // i.e. distributing the fees to well-behaved LPs, improving swap pricing, etc␊
    contract MyHook is AntiSandwichHook, ERC20 {␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager)␊
            BaseHook(_poolManager)␊
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")␊
        {}␊
    ␊
        function _afterSwapHandler(PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta, uint256 targetUnspecifiedAmount, uint256 feeAmount)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the accumulated penalty fees from sandwich attacks are handled after swaps␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96)␊
            internal␊
            override␊

        }␊

            // TODO: Implement __beforeAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊

            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊

            // TODO: Implement __beforeRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeDonate␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊

## currency settler AntiSandwichHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {AntiSandwichHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/general/AntiSandwichHook.sol";␊
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {Currency} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/Currency.sol";␊
    import {CurrencySettler} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/utils/CurrencySettler.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    ␊
    // TODO: Override \`_afterSwapHandler\` to determine how accumulated penalty fees are handled␊
    // i.e. distributing the fees to well-behaved LPs, improving swap pricing, etc␊
    contract MyHook is AntiSandwichHook, ERC20 {␊
        using CurrencySettler for Currency;␊
    ␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager)␊
            BaseHook(_poolManager)␊
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")␊
        {}␊
    ␊
        function _afterSwapHandler(PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta, uint256 targetUnspecifiedAmount, uint256 feeAmount)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the accumulated penalty fees from sandwich attacks are handled after swaps␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96, int24 tick)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeDonate␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: false,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: true,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: false,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: false␊
            });␊
        }␊
    }␊
    `

## access control (roles) AntiSandwichHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {AccessControl} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/AccessControl.sol";␊
    import {AntiSandwichHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/general/AntiSandwichHook.sol";␊
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊

        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeDonate␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: false,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: true,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: false,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: false␊
            });␊
        }␊
    }␊
    `

## pausable AntiSandwichHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {AntiSandwichHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/general/AntiSandwichHook.sol";␊
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {BeforeSwapDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BeforeSwapDelta.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {Ownable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable.sol";␊
    import {Pausable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/utils/Pausable.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    ␊
    // TODO: Override \`_afterSwapHandler\` to determine how accumulated penalty fees are handled␊
    // i.e. distributing the fees to well-behaved LPs, improving swap pricing, etc␊
    contract MyHook is AntiSandwichHook, ERC20, Pausable, Ownable {␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address initialOwner)␊
            BaseHook(_poolManager)␊
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")␊
            Ownable(initialOwner)␊
        {}␊
    ␊
        function _afterSwapHandler(PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta, uint256 targetUnspecifiedAmount, uint256 feeAmount)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the accumulated penalty fees from sandwich attacks are handled after swaps␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function pause() public onlyOwner {␊
            _pause();␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function unpause() public onlyOwner {␊
            _unpause();␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            return super._beforeAddLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            return super._beforeRemoveLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)␊
        {␊
            return super._beforeSwap(sender, key, params, hookData);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            return super._beforeDonate(sender, key, amount0, amount1, hookData);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96, int24 tick)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: false,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: true,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: false,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: false,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: false␊
            });␊
        }␊
    }␊
    `

## basic LiquidityPenaltyHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {BeforeSwapDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BeforeSwapDelta.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {LiquidityPenaltyHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/general/LiquidityPenaltyHook.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    ␊
    // TODO: Determine the block number offset for the liquidity penalty␊
    // i.e. \`10\` in order to deter JIT attacks linearly for the first 10 blocks after adding liquidity␊
    contract MyHook is LiquidityPenaltyHook, ERC20 {␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager)␊
            BaseHook(_poolManager)␊
            LiquidityPenaltyHook(10)␊

        {}␊

            // TODO: Implement __beforeInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊

        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeSwap␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊

        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterSwap␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊

                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: true,␊
