## mixed permissions LiquidityPenaltyHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {BeforeSwapDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BeforeSwapDelta.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {LiquidityPenaltyHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/general/LiquidityPenaltyHook.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    ␊
    // TODO: Determine the block number offset for the liquidity penalty␊
    // i.e. \`10\` in order to deter JIT attacks linearly for the first 10 blocks after adding liquidity␊
    contract MyHook is LiquidityPenaltyHook, ERC20 {␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager)␊
            BaseHook(_poolManager)␊
            LiquidityPenaltyHook(10)␊
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")␊
        {}␊
    ␊
        function _beforeInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeSwap␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeDonate␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: false,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: false,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: false,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: false,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: false,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: true␊
            });␊
        }␊
    }␊
    `

## safeCast LiquidityPenaltyHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊

## transient storage LiquidityPenaltyHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {BeforeSwapDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BeforeSwapDelta.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {LiquidityPenaltyHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/general/LiquidityPenaltyHook.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {SlotDerivation} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/utils/SlotDerivation.sol";␊
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {TransientSlot} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/utils/TransientSlot.sol";␊
    ␊
    // TODO: Determine the block number offset for the liquidity penalty␊
    // i.e. \`10\` in order to deter JIT attacks linearly for the first 10 blocks after adding liquidity␊
    contract MyHook is LiquidityPenaltyHook, ERC20 {␊
        using SlotDerivation for bytes32;␊
        using TransientSlot for bytes32;␊
    ␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager)␊
            BaseHook(_poolManager)␊
            LiquidityPenaltyHook(10)␊
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")␊
        {}␊
    ␊
        function _beforeInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96, int24 tick)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊

            override␊

            // TODO: Implement __beforeRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeSwap␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, int128)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterSwap␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeDonate␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊

                afterSwap: true,␊

                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: true␊

## access control (ownable) LiquidityPenaltyHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {BeforeSwapDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BeforeSwapDelta.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {LiquidityPenaltyHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/general/LiquidityPenaltyHook.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {Ownable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    ␊
    // TODO: Determine the block number offset for the liquidity penalty␊
    // i.e. \`10\` in order to deter JIT attacks linearly for the first 10 blocks after adding liquidity␊
    contract MyHook is LiquidityPenaltyHook, Ownable, ERC20 {␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address initialOwner)␊
            BaseHook(_poolManager)␊
            LiquidityPenaltyHook(10)␊
            Ownable(initialOwner)␊
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")␊
        {}␊
    ␊
        function _beforeInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96, int24 tick)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊

            // TODO: Implement __beforeAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊

            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeSwap␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, int128)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterSwap␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeDonate␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: true,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: false,␊

                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: true␊

## access control (roles) LiquidityPenaltyHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {AccessControl} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/AccessControl.sol";␊
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {BeforeSwapDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BeforeSwapDelta.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {LiquidityPenaltyHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/general/LiquidityPenaltyHook.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    ␊
    // TODO: Determine the block number offset for the liquidity penalty␊
    // i.e. \`10\` in order to deter JIT attacks linearly for the first 10 blocks after adding liquidity␊
    contract MyHook is LiquidityPenaltyHook, AccessControl, ERC20 {␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address defaultAdmin)␊
            BaseHook(_poolManager)␊
            LiquidityPenaltyHook(10)␊
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")␊
        {␊
            _grantRole(DEFAULT_ADMIN_ROLE, defaultAdmin);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96, int24 tick)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeSwap␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, int128)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterSwap␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeDonate␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: true,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: false,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: true␊
            });␊

    }␊

## pausable LiquidityPenaltyHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {BeforeSwapDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BeforeSwapDelta.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {LiquidityPenaltyHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/general/LiquidityPenaltyHook.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {Ownable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable.sol";␊
    import {Pausable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/utils/Pausable.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    ␊
    // TODO: Determine the block number offset for the liquidity penalty␊
    // i.e. \`10\` in order to deter JIT attacks linearly for the first 10 blocks after adding liquidity␊
    contract MyHook is LiquidityPenaltyHook, ERC20, Pausable, Ownable {␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address initialOwner)␊
            BaseHook(_poolManager)␊
            LiquidityPenaltyHook(10)␊
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")␊
            Ownable(initialOwner)␊
        {}␊
    ␊
        function pause() public onlyOwner {␊
            _pause();␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function unpause() public onlyOwner {␊
            _unpause();␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            return super._beforeAddLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            return super._beforeRemoveLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)␊
        {␊
            return super._beforeSwap(sender, key, params, hookData);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            return super._beforeDonate(sender, key, amount0, amount1, hookData);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96, int24 tick)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, int128)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterSwap␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: true,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: false,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: true␊
            });␊
        }␊
    }␊
    `

## shares erc20 LiquidityPenaltyHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊

            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeSwap␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, int128)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterSwap␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeDonate␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: true,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: false,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: true␊
            });␊
        }␊
    }␊

## shares erc1155 LiquidityPenaltyHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {BeforeSwapDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BeforeSwapDelta.sol";␊
    import {ERC1155} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC1155/ERC1155.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {LiquidityPenaltyHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/general/LiquidityPenaltyHook.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    ␊
    // TODO: Determine the block number offset for the liquidity penalty␊
    // i.e. \`10\` in order to deter JIT attacks linearly for the first 10 blocks after adding liquidity␊
    contract MyHook is LiquidityPenaltyHook, ERC1155 {␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager)␊
            BaseHook(_poolManager)␊
            LiquidityPenaltyHook(10)␊
            ERC1155("https://example.com/metadata/{id}.json")␊
        {}␊
    ␊
        function _beforeInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96, int24 tick)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeSwap␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, int128)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterSwap␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeDonate␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: true,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: false,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: true␊
            });␊
        }␊
    }␊
    `

## basic LimitOrderHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";␊

    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    ␊
    contract MyHook is LimitOrderHook, ERC20 {␊

        }␊

            // TODO: Implement __afterRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊

            internal␊

## all permissions LimitOrderHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {BeforeSwapDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BeforeSwapDelta.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {LimitOrderHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/general/LimitOrderHook.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    ␊

        {}␊

            // TODO: Implement __beforeAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊

            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta0, BalanceDelta delta1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊

            // TODO: Implement __afterAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊

            // TODO: Implement __afterRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeSwap␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊

        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterDonate␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: true,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: true,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: true␊
            });␊
        }␊
    }␊

## currency settler LimitOrderHook

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊

## transient storage LimitOrderHook

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊

## access control (roles) LimitOrderHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {AccessControl} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/AccessControl.sol";␊
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {BeforeSwapDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BeforeSwapDelta.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {LimitOrderHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/general/LimitOrderHook.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    ␊
    contract MyHook is LimitOrderHook, AccessControl, ERC20 {␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address defaultAdmin)␊
            BaseHook(_poolManager)␊
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")␊
        {␊
            _grantRole(DEFAULT_ADMIN_ROLE, defaultAdmin);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta0, BalanceDelta delta1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, BalanceDelta)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta0, BalanceDelta delta1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, BalanceDelta)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeSwap␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeDonate␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: true,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: false,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: true␊
            });␊
        }␊
    }␊

## access control (managed) LimitOrderHook

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊

    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊

## pausable LimitOrderHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {BeforeSwapDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BeforeSwapDelta.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {LimitOrderHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/general/LimitOrderHook.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {OrderIdLibrary} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/general/LimitOrderHook.sol";␊
    import {Ownable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable.sol";␊
    import {Pausable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/utils/Pausable.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    ␊
    contract MyHook is LimitOrderHook, ERC20, Pausable, Ownable {␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address initialOwner)␊
            BaseHook(_poolManager)␊
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")␊
            Ownable(initialOwner)␊
        {}␊
    ␊
        function pause() public onlyOwner {␊
            _pause();␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function unpause() public onlyOwner {␊
            _unpause();␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            return super._beforeAddLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            return super._beforeRemoveLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)␊
        {␊
            return super._beforeSwap(sender, key, params, hookData);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            return super._beforeDonate(sender, key, amount0, amount1, hookData);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function placeOrder(PoolKey calldata key, int24 tick, bool zeroForOne, uint128 liquidity)␊
            public␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
        {␊
            super.placeOrder(key, tick, zeroForOne, liquidity);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function cancelOrder(PoolKey calldata key, int24 tickLower, bool zeroForOne, address to)␊
            public␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
        {␊
            super.cancelOrder(key, tickLower, zeroForOne, to);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function withdraw(OrderIdLibrary.OrderId orderId, address to)␊
            public␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (uint256, uint256)␊
        {␊
            return super.withdraw(orderId, to);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta0, BalanceDelta delta1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, BalanceDelta)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta0, BalanceDelta delta1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, BalanceDelta)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: true,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: false,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: true␊
            });␊
        }␊
    }␊
    `

## shares erc6909 LimitOrderHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {BeforeSwapDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BeforeSwapDelta.sol";␊
    import {ERC6909} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC6909/draft-ERC6909.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {LimitOrderHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/general/LimitOrderHook.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    ␊
    contract MyHook is LimitOrderHook, ERC6909 {␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager) BaseHook(_poolManager) {}␊
    ␊
        function _beforeInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta0, BalanceDelta delta1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, BalanceDelta)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta0, BalanceDelta delta1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, BalanceDelta)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeSwap␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeDonate␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: true,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: false,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: true␊
            });␊
        }␊
    }␊
    `

## basic ReHypothecationHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {Currency} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/Currency.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {ReHypothecationHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/general/ReHypothecationHook.sol";␊
    ␊
    // TODO: Override the required functions to customize the rehypothecation logic␊
    // i.e. keeping the liquidity in a yield-bearing ERC-4626 Vault while still being available for swaps, etc␊
    contract MyHook is ReHypothecationHook {␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager)␊
            BaseHook(_poolManager)␊
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")␊
        {}␊
    ␊
        function getCurrencyYieldSource(Currency currency)␊
            public␊
            view␊
            override␊
            returns (address)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the yield source address is computed for a given currency␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _depositToYieldSource(Currency currency, uint256 amount)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how a given currency is deposited to it's corresponding yield source␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _withdrawFromYieldSource(Currency currency, uint256 amount)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how a given currency is withdrawn from it's corresponding yield source␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _getAmountInYieldSource(Currency currency)␊
            internal␊
            view␊
            override␊
            returns (uint256)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the hook's balance of a given currency in it's corresponding yield source is obtained␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96, int24 tick)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta0, BalanceDelta delta1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, BalanceDelta)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta0, BalanceDelta delta1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, BalanceDelta)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeDonate␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: true,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: false,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: true␊
            });␊
        }␊
    }␊
    `

## currency settler ReHypothecationHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {Currency} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/Currency.sol";␊
    import {CurrencySettler} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/utils/CurrencySettler.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {ReHypothecationHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/general/ReHypothecationHook.sol";␊
    ␊
    // TODO: Override the required functions to customize the rehypothecation logic␊
    // i.e. keeping the liquidity in a yield-bearing ERC-4626 Vault while still being available for swaps, etc␊
    contract MyHook is ReHypothecationHook {␊
        using CurrencySettler for Currency;␊
    ␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager)␊
            BaseHook(_poolManager)␊
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")␊
        {}␊
    ␊
        function getCurrencyYieldSource(Currency currency)␊
            public␊
            view␊
            override␊
            returns (address)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the yield source address is computed for a given currency␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _depositToYieldSource(Currency currency, uint256 amount)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how a given currency is deposited to it's corresponding yield source␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _withdrawFromYieldSource(Currency currency, uint256 amount)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how a given currency is withdrawn from it's corresponding yield source␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _getAmountInYieldSource(Currency currency)␊
            internal␊
            view␊
            override␊
            returns (uint256)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the hook's balance of a given currency in it's corresponding yield source is obtained␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96, int24 tick)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta0, BalanceDelta delta1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, BalanceDelta)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta0, BalanceDelta delta1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, BalanceDelta)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeDonate␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: true,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: false,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: true␊
            });␊
        }␊
    }␊
    `

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊

## access control (roles) ReHypothecationHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {AccessControl} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/AccessControl.sol";␊
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {Currency} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/Currency.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {ReHypothecationHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/general/ReHypothecationHook.sol";␊
    ␊
    // TODO: Override the required functions to customize the rehypothecation logic␊
    // i.e. keeping the liquidity in a yield-bearing ERC-4626 Vault while still being available for swaps, etc␊
    contract MyHook is ReHypothecationHook, AccessControl {␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address defaultAdmin)␊
            BaseHook(_poolManager)␊
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")␊
        {␊
            _grantRole(DEFAULT_ADMIN_ROLE, defaultAdmin);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getCurrencyYieldSource(Currency currency)␊
            public␊
            view␊
            override␊
            returns (address)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the yield source address is computed for a given currency␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _depositToYieldSource(Currency currency, uint256 amount)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how a given currency is deposited to it's corresponding yield source␊
        }␊
    ␊

            internal␊
            override␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how a given currency is withdrawn from it's corresponding yield source␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _getAmountInYieldSource(Currency currency)␊
            internal␊
            view␊
            override␊
            returns (uint256)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the hook's balance of a given currency in it's corresponding yield source is obtained␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96, int24 tick)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊

        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta0, BalanceDelta delta1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, BalanceDelta)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta0, BalanceDelta delta1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊

        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊

        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: true,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: false,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: true␊
            });␊

## access control (managed) ReHypothecationHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {AccessManaged} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/manager/AccessManaged.sol";␊
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {Currency} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/Currency.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {ReHypothecationHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/general/ReHypothecationHook.sol";␊
    ␊
    // TODO: Override the required functions to customize the rehypothecation logic␊
    // i.e. keeping the liquidity in a yield-bearing ERC-4626 Vault while still being available for swaps, etc␊
    contract MyHook is ReHypothecationHook, AccessManaged {␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address initialAuthority)␊
            BaseHook(_poolManager)␊
            AccessManaged(initialAuthority)␊
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")␊
        {}␊
    ␊
        function getCurrencyYieldSource(Currency currency)␊
            public␊
            view␊
            override␊
            returns (address)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the yield source address is computed for a given currency␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _depositToYieldSource(Currency currency, uint256 amount)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how a given currency is deposited to it's corresponding yield source␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _withdrawFromYieldSource(Currency currency, uint256 amount)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how a given currency is withdrawn from it's corresponding yield source␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _getAmountInYieldSource(Currency currency)␊
            internal␊
            view␊
            override␊
            returns (uint256)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the hook's balance of a given currency in it's corresponding yield source is obtained␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96, int24 tick)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta0, BalanceDelta delta1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, BalanceDelta)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta0, BalanceDelta delta1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, BalanceDelta)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeDonate␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: true,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: false,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: true␊

## pausable ReHypothecationHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {BeforeSwapDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BeforeSwapDelta.sol";␊
    import {Currency} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/Currency.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {Ownable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable.sol";␊
    import {Pausable} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/utils/Pausable.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {ReHypothecationHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/general/ReHypothecationHook.sol";␊
    import {SwapParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    ␊
    // TODO: Override the required functions to customize the rehypothecation logic␊
    // i.e. keeping the liquidity in a yield-bearing ERC-4626 Vault while still being available for swaps, etc␊
    contract MyHook is ReHypothecationHook, Pausable, Ownable {␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager, address initialOwner)␊
            BaseHook(_poolManager)␊
            ERC20("MyShares", "MSH")␊
            Ownable(initialOwner)␊
        {}␊
    ␊
        function getCurrencyYieldSource(Currency currency)␊
            public␊
            view␊
            override␊
            returns (address)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the yield source address is computed for a given currency␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _depositToYieldSource(Currency currency, uint256 amount)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how a given currency is deposited to it's corresponding yield source␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _withdrawFromYieldSource(Currency currency, uint256 amount)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how a given currency is withdrawn from it's corresponding yield source␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _getAmountInYieldSource(Currency currency)␊
            internal␊
            view␊
            override␊
            returns (uint256)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the hook's balance of a given currency in it's corresponding yield source is obtained␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function pause() public onlyOwner {␊
            _pause();␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function unpause() public onlyOwner {␊
            _unpause();␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            return super._beforeAddLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            return super._beforeRemoveLiquidity(sender, key, params, hookData);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeSwap(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, SwapParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (bytes4, BeforeSwapDelta, uint24)␊
        {␊
            return super._beforeSwap(sender, key, params, hookData);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeDonate(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint256 amount0, uint256 amount1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            return super._beforeDonate(sender, key, amount0, amount1, hookData);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function addReHypothecatedLiquidity(uint256 shares)␊
            public␊
            payable␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (BalanceDelta)␊
        {␊
            return super.addReHypothecatedLiquidity(shares);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function removeReHypothecatedLiquidity(uint256 shares)␊
            public␊
            override␊
            whenNotPaused␊
            returns (BalanceDelta)␊
        {␊
            return super.removeReHypothecatedLiquidity(shares);␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96, int24 tick)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta0, BalanceDelta delta1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, BalanceDelta)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta0, BalanceDelta delta1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4, BalanceDelta)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊
            return Hooks.Permissions({␊
                beforeInitialize: true,␊
                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidity: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeSwap: true,␊
                afterSwap: true,␊
                beforeDonate: true,␊
                afterDonate: false,␊
                beforeSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterSwapReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterAddLiquidityReturnDelta: true,␊
                afterRemoveLiquidityReturnDelta: true␊
            });␊
        }␊
    }␊
    `

        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊

        }␊
    ␊

            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊

        }␊
    ␊
        function getHookPermissions()␊
            public␊
            pure␊
            override␊
            returns (Hooks.Permissions memory)␊
        {␊

                afterInitialize: true,␊
                beforeAddLiquidity: true,␊
                beforeRemoveLiquidity: true,␊

## shares erc6909 ReHypothecationHook

> Snapshot 1

    `// SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT␊
    // Compatible with OpenZeppelin Contracts ^5.4.0 and OpenZeppelin Uniswap Hooks ^1.2.0␊
    pragma solidity ^0.8.27;␊
    ␊
    import {BalanceDelta} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/BalanceDelta.sol";␊
    import {BaseHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/base/BaseHook.sol";␊
    import {Currency} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/Currency.sol";␊
    import {ERC20} from "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";␊
    import {Hooks} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/libraries/Hooks.sol";␊
    import {IPoolManager} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/interfaces/IPoolManager.sol";␊
    import {ModifyLiquidityParams} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolOperation.sol";␊
    import {PoolKey} from "@uniswap/v4-core/src/types/PoolKey.sol";␊
    import {ReHypothecationHook} from "@openzeppelin/uniswap-hooks/general/ReHypothecationHook.sol";␊
    ␊
    // TODO: Override the required functions to customize the rehypothecation logic␊
    // i.e. keeping the liquidity in a yield-bearing ERC-4626 Vault while still being available for swaps, etc␊
    contract MyHook is ReHypothecationHook {␊
        constructor(IPoolManager _poolManager) BaseHook(_poolManager) ERC20("", "") {}␊
    ␊
        function getCurrencyYieldSource(Currency currency)␊
            public␊

        }␊

            internal␊
            view␊
            override␊
            returns (uint256)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement how the hook's balance of a given currency in it's corresponding yield source is obtained␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterInitialize(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, uint160 sqrtPriceX96, int24 tick)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterInitialize␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _beforeRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊
        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __beforeRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterAddLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta0, BalanceDelta delta1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊
            override␊

        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterAddLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊
        function _afterRemoveLiquidity(address sender, PoolKey calldata key, ModifyLiquidityParams calldata params, BalanceDelta delta0, BalanceDelta delta1, bytes calldata hookData)␊
            internal␊

        {␊
            // TODO: Implement __afterRemoveLiquidity␊
        }␊
    ␊

            internal␊
            override␊
            returns (bytes4)␊

            // TODO: Implement __beforeDonate␊

    ␊
